\DoxyCodeLine{1329         \textcolor{comment}{// Copy characters since last escaped sequence}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1331         memmove(write, last, written);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1332         write += written;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1333 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1334         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (*read++ == 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1335         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1336             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1337         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1338 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1339         \textcolor{comment}{// jsmn already checked that all escape sequences are valid}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1341         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1342         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)"{}'}: *write++ = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)"{}'}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1343         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'/'}:  *write++ = \textcolor{charliteral}{'/'};  \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1344         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)'}: *write++ = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)'}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}

\DoxyCodeLine{1346         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'f'}:  *write++ = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)f'}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1347         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'r'}:  *write++ = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)r'}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1348         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'n'}:  *write++ = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)n'}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1349         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'t'}:  *write++ = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)t'}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1350         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'u'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{1351         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1352             \textcolor{comment}{// UCS-\/2 codepoint \(\backslash\)uXXXX to UTF-\/8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1353             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} character = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1354             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (cgltf\_size i = 0; i < 4; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1355             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1356                 character = (character << 4) + cgltf\_unhex(*read++);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1357             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1358 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1359             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (character <= 0x7F)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1360             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1361                 *write++ = character \& 0xFF;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1362             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1363             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (character <= 0x7FF)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1364             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1365                 *write++ = 0xC0 | ((character >> 6) \& 0xFF);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1366                 *write++ = 0x80 | (character \& 0x3F);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1367             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1368             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1369             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1370                 *write++ = 0xE0 | ((character >> 12) \& 0xFF);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1371                 *write++ = 0x80 | ((character >> 6) \& 0x3F);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1372                 *write++ = 0x80 | (character \& 0x3F);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1373             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1374             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1375         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1376         \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{1377             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1378         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1379 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1380         last = read;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1381         read += strcspn(read, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{1382     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1383 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1384     *write = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1385     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} write -\/ string;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1386 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2045 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} cgltf\_node\_transform\_local(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcgltf__node}{cgltf\_node}}* node, cgltf\_float* out\_matrix)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2046 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2047     cgltf\_float* lm = out\_matrix;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2048 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2049     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (node-\/>has\_matrix)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2050     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2051         memcpy(lm, node-\/>matrix, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float}) * 16);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2052     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2053     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2054     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2055         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} tx = node-\/>translation[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2056         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} ty = node-\/>translation[1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2057         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} tz = node-\/>translation[2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2058 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2059         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} qx = node-\/>rotation[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2060         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} qy = node-\/>rotation[1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2061         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} qz = node-\/>rotation[2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2062         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} qw = node-\/>rotation[3];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2063 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2064         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} sx = node-\/>scale[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2065         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} sy = node-\/>scale[1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2066         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} sz = node-\/>scale[2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2067 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2068         lm[0] = (1 -\/ 2 * qy*qy -\/ 2 * qz*qz) * sx;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2069         lm[1] = (2 * qx*qy + 2 * qz*qw) * sx;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2070         lm[2] = (2 * qx*qz -\/ 2 * qy*qw) * sx;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2071         lm[3] = 0.f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2072 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2073         lm[4] = (2 * qx*qy -\/ 2 * qz*qw) * sy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2074         lm[5] = (1 -\/ 2 * qx*qx -\/ 2 * qz*qz) * sy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2075         lm[6] = (2 * qy*qz + 2 * qx*qw) * sy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2076         lm[7] = 0.f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2077 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2078         lm[8] = (2 * qx*qz + 2 * qy*qw) * sz;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2079         lm[9] = (2 * qy*qz -\/ 2 * qx*qw) * sz;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2080         lm[10] = (1 -\/ 2 * qx*qx -\/ 2 * qy*qy) * sz;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2081         lm[11] = 0.f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2082 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2083         lm[12] = tx;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2084         lm[13] = ty;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2085         lm[14] = tz;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2086         lm[15] = 1.f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2087     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2088 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2089 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2090 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} cgltf\_node\_transform\_world(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcgltf__node}{cgltf\_node}}* node, cgltf\_float* out\_matrix)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2091 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2092     cgltf\_float* lm = out\_matrix;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2093     cgltf\_node\_transform\_local(node, lm);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2094 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2095     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structcgltf__node}{cgltf\_node}}* parent = node-\/>parent;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2096 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2097     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (parent)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2098     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2099         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} pm[16];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2100         cgltf\_node\_transform\_local(parent, pm);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2101 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2102         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; i < 4; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2103         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2104             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} l0 = lm[i * 4 + 0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2105             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} l1 = lm[i * 4 + 1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2106             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} l2 = lm[i * 4 + 2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2107 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2108             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} r0 = l0 * pm[0] + l1 * pm[4] + l2 * pm[8];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2109             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} r1 = l0 * pm[1] + l1 * pm[5] + l2 * pm[9];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2110             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} r2 = l0 * pm[2] + l1 * pm[6] + l2 * pm[10];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2111 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2112             lm[i * 4 + 0] = r0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2113             lm[i * 4 + 1] = r1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2114             lm[i * 4 + 2] = r2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2115         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2116 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2117         lm[12] += pm[12];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2118         lm[13] += pm[13];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2119         lm[14] += pm[14];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2120 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2121         parent = parent-\/>parent;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2122     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2123 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3184 \textcolor{keyword}{static} cgltf\_component\_type cgltf\_json\_to\_component\_type(jsmntok\_t \textcolor{keyword}{const}* tok, \textcolor{keyword}{const} uint8\_t* json\_chunk)}

\DoxyCodeLine{5865 cgltf\_size cgltf\_num\_components(cgltf\_type type) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5866     \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (type)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5867     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5868     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} cgltf\_type\_vec2:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5869         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5870     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} cgltf\_type\_vec3:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5871         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5872     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} cgltf\_type\_vec4:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5873         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5874     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} cgltf\_type\_mat2:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5875         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5876     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} cgltf\_type\_mat3:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5877         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 9;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5878     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} cgltf\_type\_mat4:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5879         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5880     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} cgltf\_type\_invalid:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5881     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} cgltf\_type\_scalar:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5882     \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5883         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5884     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5885 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5887 \textcolor{keyword}{static} cgltf\_size cgltf\_component\_size(cgltf\_component\_type component\_type) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5888     \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (component\_type)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5889     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5890     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} cgltf\_component\_type\_r\_8:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5891     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} cgltf\_component\_type\_r\_8u:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5892         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5893     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} cgltf\_component\_type\_r\_16:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5894     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} cgltf\_component\_type\_r\_16u:}

\DoxyCodeLine{5896     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} cgltf\_component\_type\_r\_32u:}

\DoxyCodeLine{5898         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5899     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} cgltf\_component\_type\_invalid:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5900     \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5901         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5902     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5903 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5904 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5905 \textcolor{keyword}{static} cgltf\_size cgltf\_calc\_size(cgltf\_type type, cgltf\_component\_type component\_type)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5906 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5907     cgltf\_size component\_size = cgltf\_component\_size(component\_type);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5908     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (type == cgltf\_type\_mat2 \&\& component\_size == 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5909     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5910         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 8 * component\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5911     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5912     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (type == cgltf\_type\_mat3 \&\& (component\_size == 1 || component\_size == 2))}
\DoxyCodeLine{5913     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5914         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 12 * component\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5915     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5916     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} component\_size * cgltf\_num\_components(type);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5917 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{6549 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} jsmn\_parse(jsmn\_parser *parser, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *js, \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} len,}
\DoxyCodeLine{6550            jsmntok\_t *tokens, \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} num\_tokens) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6551     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6552     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6553     jsmntok\_t *token;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6554     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} count = parser-\/>toknext;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6555 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6556     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; parser-\/>pos < len \&\& js[parser-\/>pos] != \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}; parser-\/>pos++) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{6558         jsmntype\_t type;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6559 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6560         c = js[parser-\/>pos];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6561         \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6562         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\{'}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'['}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{6563             count++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6564             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tokens == NULL) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6565                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6566             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6567             token = jsmn\_alloc\_token(parser, tokens, num\_tokens);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6568             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (token == NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6569                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} JSMN\_ERROR\_NOMEM;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6570             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (parser-\/>toksuper != -\/1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6571                 tokens[parser-\/>toksuper].size++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6572 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef JSMN\_PARENT\_LINKS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6573                 token-\/>parent = parser-\/>toksuper;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6574 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6575             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6576             token-\/>type = (c == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\{'} ? JSMN\_OBJECT : JSMN\_ARRAY);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6577             token-\/>start = parser-\/>pos;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6578             parser-\/>toksuper = parser-\/>toknext -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6579             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6580         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\}'}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{']'}:}

\DoxyCodeLine{6582                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6583             type = (c == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\}'} ? JSMN\_OBJECT : JSMN\_ARRAY);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6584 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef JSMN\_PARENT\_LINKS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6585             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (parser-\/>toknext < 1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6586                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} JSMN\_ERROR\_INVAL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6587             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6588             token = \&tokens[parser-\/>toknext -\/ 1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6589             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (;;) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6590                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (token-\/>start != -\/1 \&\& token-\/>end == -\/1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6591                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (token-\/>type != type) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6592                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} JSMN\_ERROR\_INVAL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6593                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6594                     token-\/>end = parser-\/>pos + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6595                     parser-\/>toksuper = token-\/>parent;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6596                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6597                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6598                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (token-\/>parent == -\/1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6599                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(token-\/>type != type || parser-\/>toksuper == -\/1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6600                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} JSMN\_ERROR\_INVAL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6601                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6602                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6603                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6604                 token = \&tokens[token-\/>parent];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6605             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6606 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6607             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = parser-\/>toknext -\/ 1; i >= 0; i-\/-\/) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6608                 token = \&tokens[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6609                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (token-\/>start != -\/1 \&\& token-\/>end == -\/1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6610                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (token-\/>type != type) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6611                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} JSMN\_ERROR\_INVAL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6612                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6613                     parser-\/>toksuper = -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6614                     token-\/>end = parser-\/>pos + 1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{6616                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6617             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6618             \textcolor{comment}{/* Error if unmatched closing bracket */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6619             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (i == -\/1) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} JSMN\_ERROR\_INVAL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6620             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (; i >= 0; i-\/-\/) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6621                 token = \&tokens[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6622                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (token-\/>start != -\/1 \&\& token-\/>end == -\/1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6623                     parser-\/>toksuper = i;}

\DoxyCodeLine{6625                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6626             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6627 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6628             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6629         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)"{}'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{6630             r = jsmn\_parse\_string(parser, js, len, tokens, num\_tokens);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6631             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6632             count++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6633             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (parser-\/>toksuper != -\/1 \&\& tokens != NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6634                 tokens[parser-\/>toksuper].size++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6635             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6636         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)t'} : \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)r'} : \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)n'} : \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{' '}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{6637             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6638         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{':'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{6639             parser-\/>toksuper = parser-\/>toknext -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6640             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6641         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{','}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{6642             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tokens != NULL \&\& parser-\/>toksuper != -\/1 \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{6643                     tokens[parser-\/>toksuper].type != JSMN\_ARRAY \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{6644                     tokens[parser-\/>toksuper].type != JSMN\_OBJECT) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6645 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef JSMN\_PARENT\_LINKS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6646                 parser-\/>toksuper = tokens[parser-\/>toksuper].parent;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6647 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6648                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = parser-\/>toknext -\/ 1; i >= 0; i-\/-\/) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6649                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tokens[i].type == JSMN\_ARRAY || tokens[i].type == JSMN\_OBJECT) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6650                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tokens[i].start != -\/1 \&\& tokens[i].end == -\/1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6651                             parser-\/>toksuper = i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6652                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6653                         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6654                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6655                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6656 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6657             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6658             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6659 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef JSMN\_STRICT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6660             \textcolor{comment}{/* In strict mode primitives are: numbers and booleans */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6661         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'-\/'}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'0'}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'1'} : \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'2'}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'3'} : \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'4'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{6662         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'5'}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'6'}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'7'} : \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'8'}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'9'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{6663         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'t'}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'f'}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'n'} :}
\DoxyCodeLine{6664             \textcolor{comment}{/* And they must not be keys of the object */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6665             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tokens != NULL \&\& parser-\/>toksuper != -\/1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6666                 jsmntok\_t *t = \&tokens[parser-\/>toksuper];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6667                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (t-\/>type == JSMN\_OBJECT ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{6668                         (t-\/>type == JSMN\_STRING \&\& t-\/>size != 0)) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6669                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} JSMN\_ERROR\_INVAL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6670                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6671             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6672 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6673             \textcolor{comment}{/* In non-\/strict mode every unquoted value is a primitive */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6674         \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{6675 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6676             r = jsmn\_parse\_primitive(parser, js, len, tokens, num\_tokens);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6677             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (r < 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6678             count++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6679             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (parser-\/>toksuper != -\/1 \&\& tokens != NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{6680                 tokens[parser-\/>toksuper].size++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6681             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6682 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6683 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef JSMN\_STRICT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6684             \textcolor{comment}{/* Unexpected char in strict mode */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6685         \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{6686             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} JSMN\_ERROR\_INVAL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6687 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6688         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6689     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6690 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6691     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tokens != NULL) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6692         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = parser-\/>toknext -\/ 1; i >= 0; i-\/-\/) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6693             \textcolor{comment}{/* Unmatched opened object or array */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6694             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tokens[i].start != -\/1 \&\& tokens[i].end == -\/1) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6695                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} JSMN\_ERROR\_PART;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6696             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6697         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6698     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6699 }
\DoxyCodeLine{6700     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} count;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6701 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6702 }
